Campaign Conference Issues Declaration 136

The declaration of the 14th Hygiene Campaign in this city states: "Shanghai, a metropolis in the East with three million residents, has the most modern buildings and the most advanced transportation. However, what are the lifestyles of the residents in this small metropolis? What is their health like? If we examine the daily or recreational lives of the citizens, we will easily find that they are living anesthetized or decadent lives of pleasure in the most irregular and unhygienic habits, gambling and dancing wildly day and night, even to the point of soliciting prostitutes, making them mentally weak and physically frail. On the other hand, many citizens struggling for a living spend their lives in the most unhygienic environments or jobs. At the same time, we absolutely cannot deny that our people are too neglectful of hygiene, or at least too inattentive to it. They almost all have traditional unhygienic bad habits. We statistically find that every year, the people's illnesses and deaths, just from tuberculosis deaths alone, number 1.6 million nationwide. This is truly a staggering number. Every time the door is opened, the first gift that foreign countries bring to our country is opium, followed by heroin, red pills, sent into our country by the thousands upon thousands. Thus, our people by the thousands upon thousands are corrupted and anesthetized. In this city, the pervasiveness of poisons is even more frighteningly vast, and countless citizens are entangled in this chronic killing poison, walking to the grave day by day. Therefore, the holding of this 14th Hygiene Campaign should be said to contain the most significant meaning. Our points of attention are divided into personal hygiene and public hygiene, and at the same time, we especially focus on the official publicity of drug rehabilitation. (1) Personal hygiene, everyone must remember the saying 'A sound mind in a sound body,' especially in this year of extreme social and economic decline, if an individual does not have a healthy body, they will never be able to overcome such a difficult environment. Therefore, personal hygiene should be paid attention to and strived for as much as possible. Bad habits that harm the body should be eliminated as soon as possible. All preventive scientific methods should be absolutely trusted. We must protect our own health and develop good hygiene habits ourselves. (2) Public hygiene, without public hygiene, there is no personal hygiene. Its impact extends to the economy and the nation, deeply and significantly. But our nation is very unfortunate, the most lacking in hygiene ethics. Spitting everywhere, dumping garbage at will, feces without management, mosquitoes and flies everywhere. To seek fundamental improvement, there is absolutely no hope of success without gathering the strength of the people. (3) Anti-Drug Publicity, the harm of uselessly persuading poisons to our health is very dangerous. We have no statistics, but we know that it directly and indirectly poisoned countless lives. Poison is prevalent throughout the country and has penetrated deeply into this city. If we do not eliminate poisons early, we will inevitably be killed by poisons in the future. This hygiene campaign pays special attention to anti-drug publicity, which is of great significance. The hygiene campaign has already had fourteen sessions, but this is not much, or it can be said that it has only just begun. The history that follows will be intertwined with human culture. Every time we hold a hygiene campaign, it is not a repetition, but to make it follow the laws of nature and evolve continuously, so it cannot avoid having new additions, and it cannot but have new additions. But on the other hand, the hygiene campaign is by no means an unrelated independent movement, but a continuous inheritance with its basic links, so it cannot avoid having the same places, and it cannot but have considerable places."

Major Theft Case Solved; Perpetrator Apprehended in Shanghai; Approved for Transfer to Jiading County Government 137

The Jiayu Commercial Bank in Jiading County was visited by thieves on the night of March 9 this year. They dug through the wall, entered, pried open the iron safe, and stole 1,000 plus several hundred yuan in cash. The bank reported the theft to the Jiading County Government Public Security Bureau, requesting investigation and arrest. The Public Security Bureau recently apprehended a suspect in the case, Zhou Cai, a native of Jiangbei. Under interrogation, he confessed to conspiring to commit the theft and stated that the mastermind was Yang Xizi, also known as Song Changfa, a native of Jiangbei, hiding at No. 55 Rongqing Lane, Dagu Road, Public Concession, Shanghai. Therefore, Jiading Public Security Bureau Detective Sun Long, accompanied by Zhou Cai, came to Shanghai by car at 6 PM the day before yesterday, reporting to the Chengdu Road Police Station, requesting assistance in the arrest. The police first ordered detectives to secretly monitor No. 55 Rongqing Lane, Dagu Road. Unexpectedly, Yang Xizi learned of this, surrendered to the police station, and was taken into custody after being questioned. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Jiading Public Security Bureau Detective Sun Bin submitted an official document requesting permission to transfer Yang Xizi for prosecution and trial according to law. According to the confession of the accomplice Zhou Cai, "At 10 PM on the night of March 9 this year, Yang Xizi, Yang's friend, and I jointly stole from the Jiading Commercial Bank. We first dug a hole in the brick wall, and Yang and others went inside, while I stood guard outside. After obtaining the money, Yang and the other two took it away, and I didn't get a cent. I went to Yang's house afterwards, so I knew his address," and so on. When questioned, Yang Xizi claimed to be in the duck and chicken business and denied committing the theft, claiming that he did not know Zhou and was being framed. The police station lawyer Qian Yi then expressed his opinion, stating that Yang had been arrested and prosecuted for assaulting a public works employee on August 18 last year, resulting in an acquittal. He was also arrested for theft on March 6 last year, but again escaped conviction and was acquitted. Now that he has been arrested for the third time, and the Jiading County Government has substantial evidence and the accomplice's confession, the police station does not object to the transfer. Judge Liu Guigui approved the transfer of Song Changfa, also known as Yang Xizi, to the Jiading County Government for investigation and trial.

Drug Manufacturing Facility Cracked Down in Yuyuan Road; Police and Japanese Inspectors Jointly Search; Proprietors Qiu Ya Yuebo and Others Arrested 138

Laozha Police Station West Detective Crow, and Chinese Detective Liu Junqing, learned that at No. 1238 Yuyuan Road, Shanghai, there was a secret large-scale morphine drug manufacturing facility established by the Japanese. Yesterday (the 13th), at about 5:30 PM, they, along with the Chief Inspector of the Japanese Consulate, Suzukawa Masaichi, the Squad Leader of Caojiadu Public Security Bureau, Long Jianpo, and a large number of detectives, secretly went to the location. It was a detached Western-style house, with a Japanese flag hanging. They immediately entered and found the facility fully equipped. Inside, there was a large box of finished morphine, four large vats of unfinished morphine, and a large amount of opium raw materials, ovens, machines, and all kinds of equipment. They immediately inventoried the items and sent people to guard them. They arrested the Japanese proprietor Qiu Ya Yuebo, Chinese shareholder Li Tianfu (36 years old, from Ningbo), assistants Bao A'er, Zhuang Haiquan, Wang Ziwu, Xu Maofeng, and five others, along with a privately-owned car (Concession license number 827), and took them all back to the police station to await transfer to the Special District Court for trial.

Accountant and Lawyer Sun Zhongyao Accused of Falsely Reporting Creditor's Rights and Breaching His Duty; Trial Opened Yesterday, Settlement Hoped For 139

Accountant and lawyer Sun Zhongyao, whose office is located on the fourth floor of 294 Edward Road, has recently been sued by Shi Yujiao, the legal representative of Xiamen Commercial Bank, through lawyer Yu Ao, to the Criminal Division of the First Special Court, accusing him of falsely reporting creditor's rights, breaching his duty, and committing fraud and breach of trust. The reasons for the lawsuit are briefly as follows: The defendant was appointed as the elected liquidator of the Fu Ning Shipping Co., Ltd. on May 4 of this year. The defendant published a public notice and convened a creditors' meeting at the defendant's office on the 10th to review the registered creditor's rights. The defendant reported the company's assets and liabilities. On June 14, the liquidator prepared a liquidation statement of Fu Ning Shipping Co., Ltd., listing assets of 174,540 yuan in national currency and total liabilities of 242,000,182 yuan and 78 cents. The company's assets were insufficient to pay off debts. The defendant not only did not apply for a bankruptcy declaration, but also ignored the plaintiff's reminder on the 16th, causing the liquidation to stall, damaging the plaintiff's huge interests. He should be punished in accordance with Article 232, Paragraph 1, Item 7 of the Company Law. Since the defendant is the liquidator, he should immediately list creditor's rights and debts based on the company's books. However, the defendant fabricated Xu Shu, resulting in compensation of 3,000 yuan for creditor's rights and a remuneration of 1,250 yuan in silver dollars, which were not found in the company's books or resolutions, thus committing the crime of fraud and breach of trust under Article 366 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang opened the Eighth Criminal Division to summon the defendant. The defendant did not appear. The plaintiff's lawyer Yu Aokui stated that because there was hope for a settlement in this case, he requested a postponement. The court approved the request.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation Fourth Anniversary Commemoration; Business Report Released; Progress Made in Technical Construction and Talent Training; Company Revenue Still Cannot Offset Expenses 140

It has been four years since the establishment of Eurasia Aviation Corporation. The General Manager of the company, Mr. Li Jingcong, in order to let the public understand the value and significance of the international aviation industry, specially released the company's business progress in the past four years on the occasion of the company's fourth anniversary.

Founding Through Many Twists and Turns 141

Eurasia Aviation Corporation was initially established in the winter of the 10th year of the Republic of China. On May 30, October 1, of that year, formal flights between Shanghai and Manchouli began, which is now the fourth anniversary. If we trace the preparations for the establishment, it started in the 17th year of the Republic of China, which is now more than six years ago. In the four years since its establishment, the Shanghai-Manchouli route was abandoned due to the Northeast Incident, and the Shanghai-Xinjiang route was temporarily suspended due to the Xinjiang coup. Therefore, the function of international air transportation between Eurasia is temporarily difficult to realize. However, the main purpose of Eurasia Aviation Corporation is the completion of the most convenient air transportation between Eurasia. In the past, water transportation between Eurasia was not convenient, such as sailing around the Cape of Good Hope because of geographical advantages. It was not convenient until the opening of the Suez Canal thanks to scientific developments. Today, air transportation between Eurasia is also not convenient if it only follows densely populated areas, wasting time and detouring around the southern coast of the two continents. It is necessary to use scientific developments, have the necessary equipment, and master special skills to make it possible to fly over the plateau of Central Asia. The opening of the Suez Canal was preempted by the Saxon people to dominate their Eastern colonies. Now that the problem of air transportation is at hand, how can our Chinese nation allow others to take the lead again in the direct flight route between Eurasia through Central Asia? This is why Eurasia Aviation Corporation must be established. However, our country's material civilization is still lagging behind. If we rely solely on domestic technology and organization to promote it, time will not wait for us. If we delay a little, others will seize the opportunity. Moreover, this matter is originally an international business, and in fact, it must be done in cooperation with others. This is another reason why Eurasia Aviation Corporation must allow German participation under the principle of utilizing foreign capital advocated by the Premier.

After the End of World War I 142

I personally witnessed the possibility of aircraft being used as transportation tools in Europe, which became increasingly concrete. I was then contemplating the establishment of air transportation between Eurasia. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, German Lufthansa also intended to discuss this matter with our country. I discussed it with its representative, Mr. Schmidt, in Beiping, and immediately suggested its implementation to the Party and State government. After receiving the key points, Mr. Schmidt immediately came south, and I was ordered to draft a contract with him. At that time, we considered the five main points of the contract: (1) The route should start from Shanghai, and we should strive to pass through Central Asia and fly directly to Europe. However, in order to leave room for flexibility, we set three routes: Shanghai-Manchouli, Shanghai-Mongolia, and Shanghai-Xinjiang, with the completion of the Shanghai-Xinjiang route (the most convenient route through Central Asia) as the ultimate goal. The organization of the joint venture should be a company subject to Chinese law. (3) The business and cooperation spirit should be handled under the principle of mutual benefit, but the Chinese share capital should account for 25%. The management rights of the company belong to the board of directors, which allocates the number of people according to the proportion of share capital. (4) The German side should provide the Chinese side with full technical and capital loans. The debts arising from the capital loans should not affect the shareholding. (5) In the early stage of the company's establishment, although the German side may be responsible for managing flight technology affairs, it should immediately start training qualified Chinese personnel in the country and Germany so that they can gradually be competent for part or all of the technical affairs.

Contract Negotiations Proceeded 143

For more than a year, there were intermittent interruptions until September of the 19th year, when an agreement was finally reached and signed by the Ministry of Communications and Lufthansa. The various points held by our side were fulfilled one by one. The company was initially established in June of the 10th year. On May 31 of the same year, it had already started the first transportation of air mail between Eurasia on its Shanghai-Manchouli route. However, the ultimate goal of the company's business is still the Shanghai-Xinjiang route through Central Asia, not the Shanghai-Manchouli route. However, because the direct flight route to the Far East planned by the United Kingdom, France, the Netherlands, and other countries had not yet been completed, the operation of the Shanghai-Manchouli route could shorten the delivery time of mail between Eurasia by about four or five days, and because it was technically easier to implement, it could be completed quickly, so it was used as a transitional route.

When the September 18th Incident Occurred 144

The passage through the three northeastern provinces was suddenly impossible. At that time, the Far East route planned by the United Kingdom, France, and the Netherlands had already taken shape. The company resolutely abandoned the Shanghai-Manchouli route and sought to open a route with the ultimate goal. However, at that time, the center of the company's technical organization was located in Beiping, the midpoint of the Shanghai-Manchouli route, so it was planned to take Beiping as the starting point and fly directly to Xinjiang to reach the Russian border. All the places along the route were planned to be Bailingmiao, Ruoshui River, Dihua, and Tacheng. Whether it was possible to fly through these areas, which are high mountains, vast deserts, and areas with harsh climates, was not clear at the time, but because the survival of the company's business was at stake, we had to make a desperate gamble.

Made a Risky Test Flight 145

In just one month, various connecting materials along the way were transported to Beiping. In June of the 10th year, I and the German pilot Lu Ci made the first test flight from Beiping. As a result, we safely arrived in Dihua in just 18 hours. The company's business was revived, and colleagues celebrated each other. Although this test flight was technically successful, it was still not economical. Therefore, it was finally decided to take Shanghai as the starting point, so that we could stop at the capital, the provisional capital, the auxiliary capital, and Lanzhou, the capital of Gansu Province, as well as Jiuquan and Hami, which are the key points in the northwest, to reach Tonghua. Not only is it more convenient to transport supplies to these places, but there must also be more business volume. As for the flight distance, it takes 18 hours to fly from Beiping to Tonghua, which takes two days, while it only takes one day to fly from Shanghai to Tonghua and use faster aircraft. Therefore, the company decided to

Change to Operate the Shanghai-Xinjiang Route 146

Which is closely related to Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Xinjiang, and the northwest. After more than a year of hard work, the various facilities and supply organizations on the Shanghai-Xinjiang route have been perfected and consolidated. It has also been officially opened to traffic for three months. Currently, the section from Lanzhou to Dihua has been temporarily suspended, but it can be restored as soon as the political situation in Xinjiang improves. In the past two years, the Lanzhou-Baotou and Ping-Guangdong routes, which have been approved by the Ministry of Communications, are not only necessary for absorbing air mail from various places when international traffic is opened in the future, but also can be used as temporary supplements when the Shanghai-Xinjiang route has not yet resumed. The company's survival is not a problem, so the future prospects are unlimited. Since the company has a substantial

Significance for Benefiting the Country 147

It lies in the construction of technology and the training of talents. This was already said to be the most central issue when negotiating the cooperation agreement with the German side. Regarding the training of qualified Chinese personnel, in addition to the fact that foreign personnel with more experience must still be hired temporarily in terms of driving, due to the special terrain and climate within each route, some mechanics, most mechanics, and some telecommunications personnel have been replaced by domestic personnel. A training department has been set up in the repair shop to continuously train mechanics and electrical personnel in grades. In addition, several trainees have been sent by German Lufthansa to practice. Recently, transportation driving training has also been started at home and abroad. There will be another article reporting on the situation. This is also a talent competition that actually benefits the country. As for

The Company's Operating Revenue 148

Still cannot offset expenses. This is a necessary process in the early stages of the aviation industry. There is also another article analyzing the essential points that must be subsidized. However, the author firmly believes that on the day the company's business is completed and international airmail is smooth, the company's profits will be guaranteed. The value and significance of the company's business, as well as its progress, have been summarized and frankly stated above. It is hoped that the people of the country will understand the necessity of the company's business and provide support, which is a great honor for all those engaged in the business.

Liu Haisu's Return to China Imminent, Arriving in Shanghai on the 25th 151

Liu Haisu, the principal of the Shanghai Academy of Fine Arts, was ordered by the government in the winter of 1933 to go to Germany to preside over the Berlin Chinese Art Exhibition, promote national culture, and communicate between Chinese and Western art. Its scale was grand, solemn, and enthusiastic, creating a new record for China's international literary and artistic movement. After the Berlin exhibition closed, Liu went to Paris, Switzerland, the Netherlands, London, and other places for exhibitions, a total of fourteen locations. Hundreds of thousands of people viewed the exhibitions, influencing the whole of Europe. Recently, although the London art exhibition has closed and many other places have requested exhibitions, Liu has declined due to time constraints. Liu has already departed from London on the 14th of last month on the German new ship "Xianghuasi Tuo" in cabin number 137 to return to China. He was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai yesterday (the 13th), but a telegram was received stating that the ship's boiler was damaged in the Suez Canal and is currently being repaired, so the arrival will be delayed until around the 25th of this month. Liu's return to China this time will surely contribute his two years of experience and observations to China's art world, revitalizing its atmosphere. Cultural groups and friends of Liu in Shanghai are preparing a warm welcome, and it is expected to be a grand occasion.

Joint Meeting of Rickshaw Pullers from Various Districts Demands Implementation of New Rules by the Mutual Aid Society and Implementation of Summer Relief Measures 152

Rickshaw pullers from various districts of the city, requesting the mutual aid society to publish ten months of accounts, implement new rules, and provide formal relief to rickshaw pullers, held a joint meeting of rickshaw pullers from various districts at 32 Qianyi Lane, Tiantong Road, Hongkou yesterday afternoon. More than 30 people including Bian Qingzhong, Dai Kerong, Chen Zhengru, and Xu Hanyuan attended. Bian Qingzhong was elected chairman and Dai Kerong was elected secretary. After formal greetings, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, rickshaw pullers from various districts stood up and reported their registration certificates and badge numbers. The chairman then put forward various important issues for discussion. Regarding the case of whether the mutual aid society's accounts should be audited, it was resolved that since the mutual aid society was organized with the donations of rickshaw pullers, who have contributed a total of seven yuan and five jiao per rickshaw over ten months (each rickshaw puller is only allowed to pull ten shifts per month, with a donation of five fen per shift, totaling seven jiao and five fen per month), a request should be made to publish all the accounts in accordance with the law. (2) Regarding the implementation of the new rules, it was resolved that rickshaw pullers should first directly negotiate with the board of directors and the mutual aid society, and then elect representatives to ask the two directors of the mutual aid society who are also rickshaw merchants to present the matter at the meeting, requesting the mutual aid society to formally implement the new rules. (3) Regarding the case of requesting the mutual aid society to provide relief to rickshaw pullers, it was resolved that in this hot weather, the mutual aid society should be requested to distribute a straw hat, a set of clothing, and a pair of straw sandals to each rickshaw puller as soon as possible, as well as distribute medicine and administer vaccinations to prevent epidemics. Furthermore, considering the summer heat, the tea stations sponsored by various mutual aid societies on the roads are still lacking. It was resolved that the above cases should be submitted to the board of directors and the mutual aid society for immediate implementation. As a temporary motion, it was decided to appoint rickshaw puller representatives to petition and negotiate with the board of directors of the Public Concession, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and the Vehicle Management Committee on issues such as vehicle fares.

Reassessment of Ren De Textile Factory's Property Tax 154

The existing factory site of the Ren De Textile Factory at 590 Linqing Road is the factory's own property. After the Public Works Department's donation office assessed the property tax, the factory considered it too high and specially requested the Public Works Department's property tax valuation committee to reassess it. According to the committee's reassessment, the property tax payable by the factory should be calculated based on an annual rent of 31,200 yuan. This matter has been reported by the Public Works Department's finance office to the board of directors for approval.

He Baosheng's Death Case Involves Innocents, Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association Sends Letters to Investigate 157

The case of He Baosheng, a coppersmith from Shaoxing working on the British Swire Company's "Lexington" ship, who died by jumping into the sea in American waters last year, has caused much speculation and the truth remains unclear. The Chinese government is investigating the matter. When the "Lexington" sailed to Shanghai this time, the Municipal Public Security Bureau was ordered to thoroughly investigate the case, and took the ship's stoker chief Tu Decai, seaman chief Jiang Fucai, and Chen Tongbei, Le A'er, etc. to the bureau for questioning. Unexpectedly, the deceased's family falsely accused the Shaoxing Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, claiming that Tu, Jiang, etc. were suspects and requesting their detention and forbidding them to work. As a result, Tu Decai, etc. were almost dismissed by the company. Fortunately, with the guarantee of the Chinese Seamen's Union and the Yan Ying General Association, they were able to regain their freedom and return to work. It is now heard that after this case occurred, the families of Tu Decai, etc. complained to the Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, seeking justice. The association, based on the relationship between fellow provincials, sent letters and dispatched Dong Xinqin to the Shaoxing Fellow-Provincials Association and the Chinese Seamen's Union to investigate. The letter to the Seamen's Union reads: "We are writing to you concerning the complaint of Tu Gao's and Jiang Xie's families from our fellow province, stating that their husbands Tu Decai, Jiang Fucai, etc. have been working as stokers and seamen on ships for a long time. They are honest and law-abiding and serve as stoker chief and seaman chief on the British Swire Company's 'Lexington' ship. Half a day ago, He Baosheng, a coppersmith from Shaoxing on the same ship, committed suicide by jumping into the sea in American waters for unknown reasons. The cause of death is unclear, and the autumn government is investigating. When the 'Lexington' sailed to Shanghai this time, the Municipal Public Security Bureau was ordered to thoroughly investigate the case, and took those involved in the work, such as Tu Decai, Jiang Fucai, Chen Tongbei, Le A'er, etc., to the bureau for questioning. Unexpectedly, the Shaoxing Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai requested the Public Security Bureau to detain them and forbid them to work based on the one-sided words of the deceased's family. Their husbands' positions were almost terminated by the company. Fortunately, the gentlemen of the Chinese Seamen's Union upheld justice and made every effort to rescue them, allowing them to regain their freedom and return to work. However, after this case occurred, not only was the reputation of their husbands harmed, but the case is still pending and may cause even greater harm. We ask you to handle this matter according to the law. We check that Jiang and Tu have been serving on ships for a long time, and they are all known to be loyal, diligent and thrifty by the workers in the seaman and stoker gangs. This time they were innocently implicated and almost lost their jobs. Fortunately, your union supported them strongly, and we, members of the association, are deeply grateful. However, the state of the case is not yet resolved and further trouble must be guarded against. Our association should pay attention to post-event matters with your union. We have sent Dong Xinqin, our staff to see you, so please give us your guidance as we ask this from Chinese Seamen's Union chairman Yang."

Shanghai Telephone Company's Telephone Directory Adopts the Four-Corner Code Indexing Method 158

Since Wang Yunwu invented the Four-Corner Code indexing method, it has been easy to learn and use, and has long been adopted by domestic party and government agencies, libraries, schools, and other public and private organizations for managing files and compiling catalogs. Many libraries, publishers, and schools in foreign countries such as the United States, Japan, Batavia, and the Malay Peninsula have also adopted this indexing method. In terms of applications to publications in China, in addition to the dozens of books published by the Commercial Press, the newly compiled Secret Code Telegram of the Ministry of Communications, the Beijing Library Bibliography Index, the Shen Bao's Republic of China New Map Index, and the Kaiming Bookstore's Ci Tong and Twenty-Five Histories Index are also arranged using this indexing method to make it easier for readers to check. It is now learned that the Shanghai Telephone Company's recently compiled and published summer telephone directory has added a Four-Corner Code Index table at the beginning in addition to the original stroke order index to improve user checking efficiency. From now on, telephone users will find it more convenient to check. In addition, there are examples of the Four-Corner Code Indexing Method before the index table, so those who have never learned the method can use it after spending half an hour or an hour.

Please review the proposal. It was resolved to send a letter to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court. It was resolved that in accordance with the National Government's unified interpretation of laws and regulations and rules for changing precedents, the association has no right to forward the request. It was resolved to hand it over to the new executive and supervisory committee members for handling. Xia Yingtang's Chauffeur Dies from Gunshot Wounds Inflicted by Thugs 161

Jin Akun, a chauffeur (37 years old, from Wuxi) working for Dr. Xia Yingtang on Fangbang Road, was suddenly attacked by four thugs at around 10 PM on the 9th of this month. The thugs broke into Jin's residence upstairs in the garage at 609 Fangbang Road. They initially asked to borrow money but soon pulled out guns and fired four shots. One bullet struck Jin's abdomen, causing him to fall to the ground with injuries. The thugs then fled. His family immediately rushed the injured man to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, the injury was fatal, and he died in the hospital at 3:15 PM the day before yesterday. His body was then sent to the Phalen Road morgue for examination. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court dispatched personnel to confirm the death. His family then transported the body back to his home on Fangbang Road to prepare for the funeral. The Laobeimen police station learned of this and immediately ordered Jiang Pingyang, the chief of the ninth district, to report to the local court for an autopsy. As the court was preparing for the examination based on the report, Jin Gu's wife suddenly submitted a petition to the court stating that she was 31 years old and from Wuxi, and had two sons and two daughters. Her husband, Jin Akun, was brutally murdered by gunshot. She requested to waive the autopsy, would voluntarily inspect the body, and asked for the arrest and punishment of the murderers to avenge the deceased. The court instructed her to wait for instructions.

Xu Huaixi Sues Concubine for Theft 162

Xu Huaixi, 49 years old, from Xizhuang Village, Fushan County, Shandong Province, learned Western gold and silver jewelry craftsmanship in Lushunkou as a child. In 1918, he established the Taixi Gold Store in Harbin and also served as the director of the Shengjin Department of the Maoye Bank, making a considerable profit. In 1919, through a friend's introduction, he met Luo Yuzhang, also known as Luo Lianzhen, a prostitute from Hunan Province, 35 years old, at the Jinsheng Bookstore in Pingkangli, Daowai, Harbin. At that time, Luo suffered from an eye disease, and Xu hired a doctor to treat her until she recovered. Luo was moved to tears and vowed to serve him with her body. Xu then spent 800 yuan to redeem Luo's freedom. The two then lived together. At that time, Xu had saved 4,600 taels of gold, which he remitted to the Jiufu Gonghang and Gongheli firm in Shanghai. Later, because Harbin declined, Xu and Luo traveled to Shanghai by boat to seek a livelihood. At this time, it was after the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, and the market was sluggish and there was no work to be found. Xu then discussed with Luo and they each returned to their hometowns to visit relatives, agreeing to meet in Shanghai again to make further plans. In 1933, Luo came to Shanghai from Hunan and went to the Tongshang Hotel on Beinicheng Bridge in the British Concession alone. At the same time, she wrote a letter to Xu, urging him to come to Shanghai. At this time, Xu happened to be ill and could not come to Shanghai as scheduled. He cursed to know that Luo eventually, due to her fickle nature, had an affair with Lu, an employee of the Tongshang Hotel. When Xu recovered from his illness and came to Shanghai, Luo's attitude had changed and she avoided meeting him. After Xu searched and visited in every way, he finally met her. Luo immediately spoke sweetly, claiming that someone was sowing discord and that it was a misunderstanding. From now on, she would never be unfaithful. Xu was deceived and deeply believed it to be true, and they resumed living together at No. 10 Jingyi Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao Street in the French Concession. After nearly five months, Luo Yuzhang suddenly claimed that the money deposited in the Gongheli firm, including interest, had reached 9,700 yuan. It would be better to withdraw it and deposit it in the Jiaotong Bank, which would be more secure. Xu believed her and withdrew the money in full and handed it over to Luo for safekeeping. Afterwards, when he asked Luo whether the money had been deposited in the bank, Luo kept prevaricating. After the two lived together for ten months, Luo developed bad intentions and stole her clothes, jewelry, important items, and savings book, fleeing without a trace. Xu immediately reported it to the French police, but they were not able to catch her. Xu had no choice but to file a self-complaint for theft against Luo with the Criminal Court of the Second Branch. The day before yesterday, the court summoned Luo, who sent lawyer Zhao Zuwei to represent her. Zhao said that the defendant had left Shanghai for other places, so the trial was suspended. Luo, on the afternoon of that day at about 5 p.m., went to the lawyer's office in Yongye Lane, Baike Road, to inquire about the progress of the trial. She was found out by Xu, who immediately reported to the French police. Detectives from the French police and the Public Concession police went to the entrance of Yongye Lane on Baike Road and arrested Luo. They then went to Luo's residence at No. 14 Pushou Lane, Ai'erjin Road, and confiscated the stolen gold and silver jewelry, savings book, and other stolen goods, bringing them back to the French police station for detention. Yesterday, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Branch. The police lawyer Yao Zhao and others requested a postponement of the investigation and requested that the lawsuit be handled. Then, according to the plaintiff Xu Huaixi's complaint about the defendant's escape, Luo Yuzhang was questioned. Luo confessed that the jewelry was all owned by the woman herself. She stammered about the rest. She also hired a lawyer to defend her. After Judge Shu Chang verified the confession, he ordered that the hearing be postponed to the 20th for further investigation. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Among them, "Understanding How to Cure Gonorrhea" is the most brilliant, with many illustrations. Each volume costs only [monetary unit unreadable, possibly jiao (角)] for printing costs. The sales locations are Yu Yongkang Clinic in Xiude New Village, Chengdu Road, and Beixin Bookstore on Simalu.

Two Women Dispute Over a Child - Scientific Testing to Be Adopted - Sent to the Forensic Institute in Zhenru for Testing 179

Chen Yipeizhen, a concubine of the late property merchant Chen Yide from Suzhou, who resided at No. 2, Jiusi Lane, Pushi Road, in the French Concession, has hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the Civil Court of the Special No. 2 District Court, accusing Chen Zhou, the main wife of Chen (who resided at No. 260, Baylor Road), and requesting a judgment to return her biological son, Xiong Guan, i.e., Nengyi. The defendant also hired a lawyer to deny that the plaintiff was the concubine of the deceased husband and that the son was her own biological child. A hearing has been held to question the various parties, as reported in this newspaper. The case was heard again yesterday by Judge Ma Yishu of the Special No. 2 District Court in Civil Division 7. Both parties and their lawyers appeared in court. First, the plaintiff, Chen Yipeizhen, stated that the defendant, Chen Zhou, had never given birth to a boy and that Xiong Guan was actually her biological child. Witnesses are present and a request was made for them to be questioned. The judge asked the defendant, Chen Zhou, why she still had not brought the child. Zhou stated that Tai Guan was indeed her own biological child, but he was young and timid and afraid of coming to court. She feared he would be frightened. Therefore, she did not bring him. At this point, the court ordered Dr. He Cuizhen, the obstetrician presented by the plaintiff, to be questioned. Dr. He testified that she had delivered the baby for Yipeizhen ten years ago, on July 21st of the 15th year of the Republic of China. Mr. Chen was not at home when the baby was born. Chen only arrived after the delivery was complete, etc. At this time, the plaintiff's lawyer presented a photograph, stating that the plaintiff in this case was the goddaughter of the defendant's lawyer. The photograph was taken by the wife of the defendant's lawyer. The third person on the right is the plaintiff, which is sufficient to prove that the defendant's lawyer is also deeply aware of the situation of the two parties. After the judge passed this photograph to the defendant's lawyer, Pan Chenge, to review, Lawyer Pan stood up and said that the photograph was genuine. Since the plaintiff has raised this point, the defense lawyer also has something to say. The plaintiff was originally the concubine of Wang Laowu, the owner of the Wang Ruiyu Tea Merchant in Suzhou. When this lawyer was a member of parliament in Beijing, Chen Yide accompanied the plaintiff to my place in Beijing. Chen suffered a wrongful criminal injustice and was sentenced to a long prison term after two trials. He invited me to defend him. I handled the appeal to the Supreme Court, which sent it back for retrial. He was then declared innocent. At that time, I did not charge him any legal fees. Chen and the plaintiff recognized me as their adoptive father. At that time, my son was a technician in the Ministry of Communications, and Chen and my son exchanged cards. Since then, the two sides have been in contact, and the plaintiff took a photo with my family, etc. After this questioning, the court considered that it was necessary to adopt a scientific method of examination to determine who Xiong Guan was born to. Therefore, it was ordered that both the plaintiff and the defendant, together with the child Xiong Guan, report to the court at 2:30 PM tomorrow (i.e., today), where bailiffs will be dispatched to accompany them to the Zhenru Forensic Institute to test their blood. The hearing will be adjourned to a later date. Upon hearing the order, the defendant Chen Zhou said to the court with tears in her eyes, "My child is my own biological child. He is unwilling to come to court. What if he gets frightened?" The judge instructed them to come to the court tomorrow and then go to your home to bring Xiong Guan to Zhenru for testing. Both lawyers were also instructed to clearly explain the matter to their clients. After the instruction, the court adjourned.

Educational News

Next Year's Education Funding - Decided by the Ministry of Education 180

Ordinary Education Expenses Will Decrease Rather Than Increase Compared to This Year - Compulsory Education and Border Regions Total 1.9 Million

-Minister of Education to Summon Department Heads to Discuss Education Funding via Telegram-

The central government has approved the national budget estimate for the 24th year, and the education funding item has increased compared to the original total amount. A reporter from the Riri News went to the relevant authorities of the Ministry of Education yesterday to inquire and learned the outline of the funding for the next year:

Ordinary Education Expenses - Decrease Rather Than Increase

According to relevant authorities, the education funding for the 24th year will increase slightly compared to this year due to the implementation of compulsory education. However, the ordinary education expense portion will decrease rather than increase. The original education funding was 16 million [currency unit unclear], but it was increased to approximately 19 million due to insufficient funds. Next year's funding, excluding compulsory education, has been slightly reduced compared to this year.

Compulsory Education Funding - A Significant Amount

The central government has approved 1.4 million [currency unit unclear] for compulsory education funding next year, and 500,000 [currency unit unclear] has been decided for border region education funding. Compulsory education requires a large amount of funding, with a first-phase budget of 50 million [currency unit unclear]. In order to actively promote it, the education authorities plan to increase the compulsory education funding to 10 million [currency unit unclear] in the 25th year.

Summon Department Heads - For Face-to-Face Discussion

According to the Riri News reporter, Minister of Education Wang Shijie went to Zhen [likely Zhenjiang] a few days ago to discuss Jiangsu Province's compulsory education funding with Governor Chen Guofu and Department Head Zhou [character unclear]hai. It is reported that Chen paid close attention to this and has [character unclear] funds specifically for compulsory education. Therefore, the results are very good. It is also learned that Wang believes this issue is of great importance. Although the order to raise compulsory education funds locally has been issued, in order to ensure practical measures, he will separately summon the heads of education departments from various provinces to Beijing for face-to-face consultations.

Shandong Province's Compulsory Education Fee - 2.8 Million Yuan 181

Establishment Fee of 600,000

(Jinan, 13th Dispatch) The Department of Education is planning to promote compulsory education. Each county will establish at least 20 short-term primary schools, all with half-day classes. There can be four classes in the morning and afternoon. The entire province will have more than 8,000 classes, requiring 4,000 teachers. The establishment fee is 6 million yuan, which will be allocated from the counties' military replenishment payments. The annual funding required is 2.8 million yuan, with the central government subsidizing half. Due to frequent disasters in Shandong, it is planned to request more subsidies from the central government. The Department of Education also plans to establish training courses to cultivate teachers. After the plan is finalized, it will be submitted to the provincial government's political affairs meeting on the 14th.

Good Opportunity for High Schools to Purchase Physics Experiment Equipment 183

Central Research Institute and others sell at half price

(Nanjing, 13th) The Ministry of Education ordered all departments and bureaus, as well as the Northeast Youth Education Relief Office, stating that the National Central Research Institute's Physics Institute's official letter roughly stated: In view of the need for domestic secondary schools to improve instrument equipment standards, the Institute has expanded the attached instrument factory to meet instrument needs outside the Institute with a portion of personnel and economy. Recently, the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees, which is responsible for cultural foundations and management, jointly decided to customize 100 sets of high school physics experiment instruments from the Institute, with a cost of 600 yuan per set, and to offer them to various levels of secondary schools in the country at half price (300 yuan per set) at its discretion. The method will be determined and announced by the two boards of trustees. The number of schools allocated is approximately one-fifth of the number of high schools nationwide. It is proposed to instruct the education departments of various provinces to order all public and private senior high schools that need to increase physics experimental equipment to submit reports to the department through the department, and then to the institute for customization. If the number of sets exceeds 100, the price per set can be reduced to 600 yuan. All instructions and price lists have been directly sent to various senior high schools, etc. With this approval, the department is instructed to immediately instruct all senior high schools to comply.

The City's Elementary Education Research Association is Established to Discuss Issues that the Ministry Needs to Study 190

Director Pan Chairs, Each Group Reports Separately, the Results of the Review are Revised and Approved by the General Assembly

The city's elementary education research association held its inaugural meeting at Wuben Girls' High School at 1:00 PM yesterday to discuss various research issues issued by the Ministry. Director Pan hosted a banquet for the attending representatives that evening to facilitate socializing. The details are recorded separately below.

Attendees

Director Pan of the City Education Bureau, Section Chief Zeng Shengdian, Supervisor Xie Enpu, Specialists Hu Shuyi and Zhou Shang, Section Member Zhang Zitang, expert members Chen Heqin, Dong Renjian, Shen Baiying, and representatives from various districts Guqian, Xu Shushen, Chen Kemei, Qian Xuanqing, Yan Zhenyu, Sheng Zhensheng, Zhang Shuqin, Lu Guanfang, Wang Wutang, Chai Zifei, and more than sixty other people attended, chaired by Director Pan and recorded by Zhou Longguang.

Chairman's Report

After the inauguration ceremony, the chairman reported, briefly stating that the city originally had an organization for the city's primary education research association. Later, due to the Ministry of Education's circular ordering provinces and cities to organize elementary education research associations at all levels, the City Education Bureau reorganized the former primary school education research association into the city's elementary education research association. Recently, the Ministry's various questions were divided into groups for preliminary research, and expert members were hired by the Education Bureau to assist in the review and submit them to today's general assembly for detailed discussion. As for the discussion method, due to the large number of issues, it would take a lot of time. To save time, there should not be too many restrictions on speakers. If there are no objections, the original plan based on the review will be passed.

Expert Opinions

Next, experts were invited to express their opinions: (1) Chen Heqin said that today is for research results and general review. The chairmen of each group should first report on the initial research situation and then be reviewed and approved by the general assembly. (2) Dong Renjian said that there should be a standard for reviewing various education reports, and then reviewing them would be more convenient. (3) Shen Baiying said that the research opinions on curriculum and administration should be explained item by item. The issues of teaching equipment are trivial and time-consuming. If there are no special intentions, they should be generally approved. If necessary, a committee should be organized.

Group Reports

After the experts expressed their opinions, each group began to report. (1) Shen Baiying reported on the research situation of the curriculum group. (2) Lu reported on the research situation of the teaching group. (3) Xu Shushen reported on the research situation of the equipment group. (4) Sheng Zhensheng reported on the research situation of the educational administration group.

Review Results

After each group reported, the review and discussion began. The research opinions of the four groups, including curriculum, teaching, equipment, and administration, totaled tens of thousands of words. The chairman presented each item for discussion, and the members expressed many supplementary and revised opinions. It was not until 6:00 PM that all the reviews and revisions were approved. At 7:00 PM, the director hosted a banquet at Wuben for more than sixty experts and representatives from various districts. During the banquet, they discussed elementary education issues with each other. At 10:00 PM, they happily dispersed.

Recently, many people have been registering, and the enthusiasm is very high. The situation is recorded separately below.

Personnel Appointed

In order to thoroughly implement the purpose of the camp with a large number of children, it is believed that it is not enough to have hygiene education experts preside over everything in order to achieve significant results. After many searches, it has been carefully appointed that Li Xuanguo will be the camp director, Li Zhaozhang and Zu Zhangqi will be the deputy camp directors, Shen Shanpei will be the director of general affairs, Hu Siqian will be the director of education, and Zu Zhangqi will be the director of hygiene. All nurses from the Gaoqiao Hygiene Office will be instructors, and Mayor Wu, Director Li, Director Pan, Dr. Zhang Wei, Sun Jiaqi, Zhou Shang, etc. will be invited as consultants. Li Xuanguo and Li Zhaozhang have been actively preparing for several days.

Pay Attention to Hygiene

The camp will pay special attention to nutrition and hygiene because most of our country's children are physically weak. Outdoor exercises, breathing fresh air, closing windows for sleep, brushing teeth, bathing, etc. will be fully trained. Body temperature measurement will be performed every morning and evening. Examinations of feces and blood, weighing groups, travel, and outdoor living activities will be held every week. In addition, there will be no art or natural science professors. The establishment of this camp is not just a children's paradise.

Enthusiastic Reports

Since registration began on the 7th, it has been very enthusiastic. It is reported that the camp will close registration on the 15th of this month. Those who wish to join can go to: (1) China Anti-Tuberculosis Association, No. 41 Chihama Road, Ai'erqi Road (East of Carter Road); (2) Shenbao, No. 205 Shandong Road; (3) Hygiene Office, No. 306 Ximenwai Xielu; (4) Infant Clinic, No. 785 Baoxing Road for registration. Late applications will not be accepted.

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 209

— (Lan Shan)

A fortune teller warned a young man, "You will have love affairs at the age of seventeen. This is not a good thing. You must be careful every step of the way and never try it. If the emperor has love affairs, he will abandon the beautiful country. If robbers pick flowers, they will definitely be caught. If ordinary people have love affairs, they will be confused, muddleheaded, and lose their minds. You must never try it."

People in Shanghai call girls "gua lao," which is a transliteration of the English word "Girl," but it is very interesting. For example, when you have good luck, are rich, and have power, why wouldn't they "gua lao" with you? When your "luck goes and thunder strikes the monument of happiness," even if you try hard, you can't "gua lao" with them.

Ginseng and cinnamon are precious medicines, but they only treat diseases and cannot prolong your life. If taking ginseng could lead to immortality, then all the emperors, wealthy merchants, and big businessmen of ancient and modern times would not die. If you understand this point, those who don't have ginseng to take can be at peace.

Peach Blossom River 210

— Mustard Seed

Peach Blossom River is a haven for beauties. This folk song has been popular in Shanghai for a long time, but where is this Peach Blossom River, known for producing beauties? I have a friend from Hunan, Mr. Liang, who told me that this river is in Yiyang, Hunan.

Yiyang is an important place on the shores of Dongting and Xiang, and the tea, rice, bamboo, and wood from the Zi River basin are all transferred and exported from here, so the area is exceptionally rich. There is a Wei Mountain southwest of Yiyang, and the Peach Blossom River originates from here. It winds for more than 50 li and flows into the Zi River. The mountains embrace green snails, and the water ripples with emerald jade. The scenery along the banks is extremely serene. In March every year, the peach blossoms bloom, and the banks are like fire and rosy clouds. The petals fall on the river, reflecting the river water into a pink color. It is no wonder that beautiful girls are produced along the river because of its spiritual energy. Mr. Liang said, "There is a saying in Hunan: 'Changsha clogs, Xiangtan umbrellas, Yiyang girls are worth choosing.'" It can be seen that the beauties on the Peach Blossom River are truly worthy of their name.

Whenever the weather is sunny and breezy, there are countless small boats on the Peach Blossom River, coming and going on the water. The people paddling are all dressed in colorful clothes, and they sing in the middle of the river from time to time, which makes the tourists yearn for it. Peach Blossom River, Peach Blossom River, it is truly a fairyland on earth.

Morning on Wangping Street 211

— Shen Qin

It is morning. The people on Wangping Street, the people in short clothes, are surging like the tide, coming! Going! They are busy, busy.

Among them are big newspaper vendors, small newspaper vendors, the wives of newspaper vendors, and children selling pancakes and fried dough sticks, braving the cold morning wind, barely propping up their tired bodies and bitter faces, passing through, grabbing the large bundles of newspapers thrown down from the newspaper office's cars, shouting as if hungry people were grabbing bread, vying for them. In a short time, the bundles were piled up on the sidewalk, then divided into small stacks, and then from small stacks into posts. Some grabbed them and stuffed them into their bags, hung them on their shoulders, and scattered to the east, south, west, and north, shouting: "Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao? Shishi Xinbao is here?"; some tied them to their bicycles, "Ding Ling Ling," and rushed out of Wangping Street like flying.

The sun scattered red light in the palace. The nearby time bell struck nine, Wangping Street, leaving some small waves, the big newspaper vendor with a pencil behind his ear, squatting on the ground, the abacus beads clicking, the head nodding again and again

This morning is like this, tomorrow, the day after tomorrow... Every morning is like this, the tide of people in short clothes, surging, - -

Country Wife 212

— Wave Light

Young man, you mustn't marry that kind of country woman, don't be angry when I say that! Although you are a man, you are not as free as I am, a woman. Miss Wang Xiaoru said this to Mr. Chun.

Mr. Chun is a sentimental writer. All his works are scattered in various newspapers in Shanghai, especially in S Town. Today, he suddenly heard Miss Wang say this, and he felt ashamed and indignant. He felt a burning pain in his heart.

Sleeping in bed at night, quietly savoring the words that Miss Wang said during the day: Is a country woman really not worthy to be my wife? Her face is still acceptable, but her feet are too ugly! She doesn't understand understanding, doesn't have a passionate attitude towards her husband, and is illiterate! This is her shortcoming! Mr. Chun thought of this and felt that the joy of life had disappeared from now on! Two lines of hot tears welled up in his eyes.

She heard her husband sob in his sleep. She thought he was having a nightmare, and she called out twice, "Chun! Chun!" Mr. Chun's sorrow changed again. Although she is a country woman, she is responsible for raising her children, she is thrifty with money, and she doesn't have romantic behavior. If he married a city woman, she would ask for this and that from her husband, which would be painful enough, right? Her husband is a poor wretch, and she can't live in poverty. Maybe she will get a divorce

Miss Wang's words were because she was too jealous, so she said such provocative words. But country women and city ladies really have their own advantages.

Poverty makes life unbearable, and heroism has long been exhausted.

Pretending to cry to others, knowing that there is nothing more unhumorous than this, so I imitate Mr. Yingdai to make a joke.

Girl A: Recently, several stinky men have been following behind me like groupies. What do you think is a good way to avoid them?

Girl B: That's easy, just follow behind them.

Mother: I want to give you six copper coins, but I think that's too much. I want to give you four, but I think that's too little. Can you help me figure out how much money I should give you?

Child: Then give me ten! Too much and too little mixed together are just right.

Old Wang: Do you know why most modern women cut their nails into sharp points?

Interesting Translations 215

— Wan

The study of translation has indeed improved now. Simple transliterations like "Ji Li, Lanxi," etc., and adding a "mouth" radical to indicate that it is a transliterated word, will no longer exist. In modern essays, many transliterated words are very fresh and meaningful! Let's take a few of the most common ones as examples. For example, "Fiance'e" in English means "fiancée." There is a transliteration that is read as "fei yang san" (廢陽傘), which means "useless umbrella." A useless umbrella is something that only has the name of an umbrella but cannot block the sun or rain. The usefulness of a fiancée is equivalent to a useless umbrella. This transliteration is very accurate. "Husband" in English means "husband." The current popular transliteration is "hei qi ban deng" (黑漆板凳), which means "black lacquered bench." Of course! Modern wives treat their husbands as benches to sit on and play with under their butts. When they feel that it is not suitable, they can kick him away and replace him with another one to sit on. It's just a little difficult to be a black lacquered bench. "Girl" in English means "girl." The current popular transliteration is read as "gou er" (狗兒), which means "puppy." Comparing a girl to a puppy is a bit inappropriate and somewhat blasphemous to women, but have you ever seen the kind of white terrier puppies that modern women or foreign women lead? It's so beautiful, so soft, so handsome! "Long Kiss" in English means a long, deep kiss. The current popular transliteration is read as "lang ke si" (郎渴死), which means "the man is thirsty to death." These three words are unspeakably wonderful. Readers can understand them beyond the words, so I don't need to explain them in detail.

Fourth Aunt 216

— Gu Feng

Now fourth aunt is sleeping forever.

Speaking of fourth aunt, I can still remember: a short, fat woman with a dark face and sparse hair on her forehead, almost the same as fourth uncle. This is because she has been married to fourth uncle for fifteen or sixteen years and has given birth to five children, obviously working too hard in childbirth! This is a special mark of educational achievement, and no one can deny it. Speaking of her voice, it was like a Hong Zhong bell, she should not be short-lived, but now she only lived to be thirty-nine years old!

When she was lying stiffly on the coffin lid, the people around her were discussing: two years ago, fourth uncle had just graduated from medical school, although he had a sign, the business was very few, so the household expenses were really a few countable coins. I remember one summer, the health bureau sent fourth uncle to the Peking Union Medical College Hospital for an internship, which was to last three months. Fourth uncle was born a rat and had no food to store for the next day. When he arrived in Peking, the family's livelihood was unsustainable. Fourth aunt asked someone to write letters to urge him, and fourth uncle had no choice but to borrow fifteen yuan a month from his cousin to cope. After the three-month internship was over, fourth uncle was assigned to work in the bureau, and he received a salary of one hundred and twenty or thirty yuan a month. Later, he was hired by a company as a medical consultant, and he could earn about two hundred in total. It's only been two years! Life gradually became abundant, and everyone thought fourth aunt could enjoy happiness, but after the Mid-Autumn Festival last year, she suddenly got hemoptysis, which was very severe. Although her own husband was a doctor, and her husband's friends were also doctors, the needles and medicines were ineffective in the end. Everyone said fourth aunt was a hard-working life!

Everyone was talking about it, no one sympathized with her for being unlucky and unable to enjoy wealth and live a long life together. But fourth aunt was just silent!

Records of the Fragrant Vapor 217

— Qing Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

Another spectacle is the yellow glazed tiles on the roofs of those large palaces, which reflect a dazzling golden light when they are shrouded in sunlight. Usually, you wouldn't see any wonders when looking at them up close. Now, on the boat, looking across the lake, it looks like a golden glow in the air.

Doesn't the Empress Dowager have two yachts prepared? The one she always rides is called the "Imperial Boat," and the other one may as well be called the "Vice Imperial Boat." Its size and style are roughly the same as the Imperial Boat, but it is not as gorgeous. And the color of the fake tiles on its cabin top is green, which is also to distinguish it from the Imperial Boat. Every time we cruise the lake, all the female officials who are not on duty to attend the Empress Dowager, as well as the lower-ranking people in the palace, all have to ride it, following closely behind the Imperial Boat, about five or six zhang away, protecting it. I don't know whether its interior arrangement and the smoothness of the boat are inferior to the Imperial Boat, because I am always on the Imperial Boat and have never ridden it.

In addition to this "Vice Imperial Boat," there are four small yachts that must also follow the Empress Dowager to the lake every time. Two are in the front, divided into left and right, and follow far behind the Imperial Boat. These are for the palace band to ride on – this is the "fine band," not the annoying "coarse band" used during rituals. — They are about twenty people in total, divided into two small boats. (339)

Commercial News

Finance Trading Approaching; Gold Market Lingering Without Honor or Disgrace 219

Recently, the gold market has seen a lack of activity from major players. Coupled with the approaching trading period, retail investors are also hesitant to speculate excessively, resulting in a dull market with unremarkable supply and demand. Yesterday's market showed initial weakness followed by strength, with overall sentiment remaining neutral, ultimately resulting in a slight increase. In the early morning, overseas silver markets contracted. However, large speculators claimed that after the market closed, Indian and local speculators bought in, causing the market to strengthen, with the final transaction price higher at 625. Mondelay forward silver prices fell slightly. Exchange rates opened higher but closed lower. London spot gold fell sharply by one shilling and one penny. News reported that the Minister of Finance responded to silver factions' silver purchases, stating that the existing order would not change. Although this is outdated, it still stimulated the psychology of general retail investors, causing over-the-counter preparatory trading to open with a lack of buyers, falling from over 70 yuan to 67.8 yuan before stabilizing and recovering. The Central Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with the British pound unchanged and the US dollar contracting. Customs gold units fell by one cent. The gold standard price was again lowered to 835 yuan. It was heard that the market remained weak afterward, but stabilized with refined gold, as short sellers moved to cover their positions and major players also came to purchase bars, gradually pulling the market up. The HSBC Bank's official exchange rates were announced, with both British pound and US dollar unchanged. Subsequently, banks hedged the US dollar and broke through the 70 yuan barrier, with supply and demand balancing. Many buy orders appeared, but the increase was limited, and the market was extremely calm, lacking special changes, mainly because the foreign exchange market process was also quiet. Helplessly, major players continued to purchase bars, and floating shorts felt disappointed. At noon, the trend became stronger again, and the after-market continued to be stable. Although there was supply at higher prices, the buying was still strong, and prices rose again. When the report of Indian silver shrinking by one anna and rising by 1.2 annas came, buyers showed some disappointment and prices declined. However, due to limited trading, there was much lingering, and after the second report of Indian silver rising by 4.2.1 annas, people were disappointed and bulls sold off, leading to a decline. Finally, there was a lack of large-scale supply and demand, resulting in a particularly sluggish state. The foreign exchange market also lacked changes. The market situation for the day is recorded below.

The morning opening price was 768.5 yuan, down 2 yuan from the previous close. Da Fa, Yongfu, and Xingyong sold off, dropping to 7 yuan and 6 jiao. Fuxing, Yongheng, Yuda Cheng, Hengchang, and Yonglai bought in, favorably hedging July US dollars at 625, rising to 9 yuan and 8 jiao. Fuxing, Yongjia, Runyuan, and Maoyong sold off at higher prices, retreating to 8 yuan and 5 jiao. Anticipating HSBC's exchange rate announcement, the British pound and US dollar were both unchanged. Yuanchang, Yongheng, and Yu bought bars and remained stable. Later, Hengyu, Tongfu, Fuxing, and Yonglai bought in, breaking through the 70 yuan barrier, rising to 70 yuan. Dade Cheng, Yifeng, and Yong sold bars, falling to 69 yuan and 4 jiao. Hengxing, Hengchang, Yongchun, and Yuanyong all bought in. Mecca and ate August US dollars at 1875, rising to 72 yuan and 3 jiao. Hengyu, Hengjiang, and Yingxiang sold off. Citibank came out with August US dollars at 875, falling to 0.5 jiao. Dull Glutinous Rice Sales Lag, Foreign Rice Stabilizes 228

Local rice (from the southern Shanghai area) yesterday was scarce in supply from various sources, with a total of eighteen shipments arriving (nearly four thousand piculs). However, in terms of sales, due to tight monetary conditions, it was difficult to see an improvement. Therefore, although urban and rural stores made some purchases, the quantity was small. Moreover, contracted purchases were suddenly suspended. As a result, the prices of various high-quality glutinous rice varieties were stable. Since there was a larger supply of late rice varieties, and sales were weak, prices were slightly lower, by a few cents to nearly a dime. Other varieties such as "Bian Yuan" and "Du Jian," were generally stable. (In the northern Shanghai area) yesterday, seventeen or eighteen shipments arrived from various routes below the river. Sales of all varieties were flat. The market price of white glutinous rice was firm, dry rice was stable, and high-quality "Bai Yuan" rice was slightly lower by a few cents; other varieties were stable.

Foreign Rice: Yesterday, the foreign rice market was initially in a strong position, but it was affected by rumors. Local rice merchants were hesitant to purchase. After continuous active purchases from inland Zhejiang province, demand was still being met. Local demand was limited, and the market showed signs of a sudden decline. Subsequently, Anqing, Hankou, and Jiujiang merchants from Nanjing and the Yangtze River region continued to purchase, and demand was strong. The market gradually recovered. Throughout the day, 10,000 bags of Saigon No. 1 and broken rice were sold, and 5,700 bags of small-grain rice were sold. It is said that the market will stabilize again.

Piece Goods: Western Tribute Cloth Already Affected 232

"Yuan Qing" tribute cloth, a popular item, sells year-round. The shoe industry is the largest customer. Recently, however, the selling price has also fallen. The reasons are: (1) new goods are cheaper due to exchange rate conditions; (2) the "Rong Tai" tribute cloth standard has collapsed, and various brands are flooding the market; (3) it is affected by the cheap dumping of Japanese "Yuan Zhi" tribute cloth and the promotion of domestic "Xian Tong Hua" tribute cloth; (4) the weather is extremely hot, sales are slow, and the shoe factories are using less due to the impact of domestic "Da Wu" cloth.

Silk and Tea: Tunxi Zhen Mei Tea Trading Brisk 233

Yesterday, Tunxi high-grade "Zhen Mei" green tea was actively purchased by British firms such as Xiehe, Jinlong, Fushi, and Baochang in response to overseas orders. Trading was brisk, but the opening price was lower by one or two yuan due to the weak negotiating power of Chinese merchants. Both British and Russian firms purchased black tea from Qimen, Fuliang, Ningzhou, and Hekou, and sales were slightly more active. The price of high-quality goods remained stable, but low-grade goods continued to fall by one or two yuan to four or five yuan.
